## Contexts in which the phrase **soviet union** was used in the House of Representatives during the 1970s

* I can inform the House that it is the normal policy of the USSR to try to ensure that countries in its immediate vicinity or close to the Russian borders give the kind of help, and according to the conditions, that might be imposed by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> itself. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19700605_reps_27_hor68/#subdebate-11-0)

* Has the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> tied strings to its help by demanding full military and economic cooperation as the price for flood damage assistance? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19700605_reps_27_hor68/#subdebate-11-0)

* A second tabled in the General Assembly by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and other Eastern European countries would have called for the prohibition of the development production and stockpiling of chemical and bacteriological (biological) weapons and the destruction of such weapons. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19700901_reps_27_hor69/#subdebate-23-2)

* Has the Prime Minister noticed reports that Malaysia's new Prime Minister, Tun Abdul Razak, has called for the neutralisation of South East Asia with guarantees from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, China and the United States of America? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19700923_reps_27_hor69/#subdebate-9-0)

* Comparable figures are not available for commitments by other countries including the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19701015_reps_27_hor70/#subdebate-34-7)

* In how many of these cases have unexplained delays occurred in securing the consent of the Soviet authorities for the nominees to leave the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1970/19701016_reps_27_hor70/#subdebate-27-1)

* I would not like to think that the Soviet authorities would impose such a meagre penalty on evildoers in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> convicted of a similar crime in relation to our embassy in Moscow. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1971/19710428_reps_27_hor72/#debate-34)

* Which is the southernmost of the islands over which sovereignty passed to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> under the terms of the treaty. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1971/19710915_reps_27_hor73/#subdebate-32-16)

* It was the second contract that the Meat Board was able to negotiate with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1971/19711013_reps_27_hor74/#subdebate-6-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is understood to have interpreted 'Kurile Islands' as including Etorofu, Kunashiri, Shikotan and the Habomais, the last being the most southerly. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1971/19711026_reps_27_hor74/#subdebate-34-5)

* The delegation from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has been to Canberra and has been entertained by the InterParliamentary Union. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720307_reps_27_hor76/#subdebate-4-0)

* I ask the Minister for Foreign Affairs: Has Australia expressed a view to Indonesia and Malaysia on the regime in the Strait of Malacca, as the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and Japan are reported to have done? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720323_reps_27_hor76/#subdebate-1-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, if you like. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720510_reps_27_hor78/#subdebate-33-0)

* Has the Minister for Foreign Affairs seen reports that Jews wishing to leave the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are being forced to pay for their freedom by being charged, on a sliding scale commensurate with their education, for their visas? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720831_reps_27_hor79/#subdebate-10-0)

* However on several occasions in the United Nations, the last occasion being at the meeting of the General Assembly last year, we have raised our voice and spoken in favour of the free movement of Jews from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> in accordance with the Universal Declaration of Human Rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720831_reps_27_hor79/#subdebate-10-0)

* We had received information that in fact the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> had been relaxing ds restriction upon the movement of Jews from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1972/19720831_reps_27_hor79/#subdebate-10-0)

* Is there any inter-departmental committee or committees dealing with any aspects of Australia's trading relations with (a) New Zealand (b) Japan (c) the United States (d) Great Britain (e) the European Economic Community (f) the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> (g) China (h) India (i) Indonesia and (j ) any other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19740918_reps_29_hor90/#subdebate-23-12)

* I cannot mention precisely at this time or in this place the countries that I shall be visiting but among them clearly will be the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> which for some time has been pressing for a visit, particularly since I have already visited the United States of America, Japan, China and Britain. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741017_reps_29_hor91/#subdebate-2-0)

* Has agreement been reached with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> for the conduct of joint research programs with Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741022_reps_29_hor91/#subdebate-52-17)

* 1 ) What action has the Government taken to assist the 3 million Jewish people in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741202_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-40-6)

* If no such action has been taken, will he raise this matter when in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741202_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-40-6)

* Will he also ask the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to end its oppression of these people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741202_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-40-6)

* What other action will he take to assist the 3 million Jewish people in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741202_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-40-6)

* Did the delegates from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> move at the International Whaling Commission meeting in London, held on 24-28 June 1974, to increase the eligible size of sperm whales to be killed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1975/19750306_reps_29_hor93/#subdebate-49-12)

* If so, did the telegram ask him to inquire about the fate of 5 Lithuanians imprisoned in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1975/19750417_reps_29_hor94/#subdebate-27-5)

* Has the Government had any reports of <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> reaction to his foreign policy statement? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1976/19760604_reps_30_hor99/#subdebate-4-0)

* The Opposition has encouraged a situation which would have helped to persuade the United States not to be involved, not to reinforce its capacities at Diego Garcia, and therefore it has encouraged a situation which would have left the Indian Ocean to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> alone. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-3-0)

* If  President  Carter can be successful in persuading the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to take its extensive naval facilities out of the Indian [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-3-0)

* Does he support the President's suggestion to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> that the super- powers should agree to demilitarising the Indian Ocean? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770310_reps_30_hor104/#subdebate-3-0)

* Today, honourable members received parcels of unleavened bread or matzah, as it is known, for forwarding to Jews in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> who are unable to get the proper bread for their celebration of the Passover this year. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#debate-29)

* This is one of the ways in which the atheistic Soviet Government persecutes all religions and I have here an account of the mean and horrible way in which it has endeavoured to deprive the Jews in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> of the ceremonial bread which they need for their celebration of the Passover. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770322_reps_30_hor104/#debate-29)

* Six days ago I drew his attention to reports from the Los Angeles spy trial that the Central Intelligence Agency was engaged in deception against Australia and that secret material involving Australia had been passed to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770503_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-14-0)

* 1 ) Has his attention been drawn to an article on page 44 of the  Bulletin  of 1 2 March 1 977 concerning the treatment of political prisoners in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1977/19770531_reps_30_hor105/#subdebate-56-1)

* Reasonable people can however reasonably conclude that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> still seeks to expand its influence throughout the world in order to achieve Soviet primacy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780223_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-8-0)

* In the last decade, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has expanded its armed forces by 1 million men. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780223_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-8-0)

* It would seem that there is an impression that the present activities of the United States are a reaction to the growing strength of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780223_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-8-0)

* There would also seem to be the impression in some places that the Government is not aware of the concerns that are aroused as a result of the growing strength of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>'s offensive forces. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780223_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-8-0)

* Kurile Islands: The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> claims, occupies and exercises jurisdiction over the Kurile Islands, which it is understood to interpret as including Kunashiri and Etorofu Islands and Shikotan Island and the Habomai group. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780308_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-30-2)

* The United States, The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, France, Britain , The Federal Republic of Germany, Canada, Japan, Switzerland, Belgium, Italy, The Netherlands, Sweden, The German Democratic Republic, Czechoslovakia and Poland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780315_reps_31_hor108/#subdebate-35-5)

* It is perhaps not surprising that the  Sydney Morning Herald,  in its brief and inadequate report of my criticisms, published the inaccurate smear of the honourable member for Eden-Monaro  (Mr Sainsbury)  that I have not opposed nuclear power in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780525_reps_31_hor109/#debate-42)

[[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19780822_reps_31_hor110/#subdebate-2-1)

* The record was evident even theft, and the rape of Hungary stands as a monument to the fulfilment of that threat by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> in the fifties- a monumental example of interference, invasion and the rape of another nation's independence. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790308_reps_31_hor113/#debate-44)

* 1 ) Has the Minister's attention been drawn to reports that the United Kingdom, the United States of America and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> have agreed to a nuclear embargo on India. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741119_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-41-26)

* Prior to the recognition of the incorporation of Latvia, Estonia and Lithuania into the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> as de jure incorporation, there was no extradition treaty in force between Australia and the U.S.S.R. Australian citizens wishing to visit the three Baltic States had to apply to a Soviet Embassy or Consulate for a visa, and a person residing in one of the three Baltic States who wished to enter Australia as a migrant had to comply with the relevant provisions of Soviet law regarding exit permits and had to apply to the Australian Embassy in Moscow for a migrant visa. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741127_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-44-17)

* After the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> seized control of the States, these treaties remained in force in theory, but in practice ceased to have any effect. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1974/19741127_reps_29_hor92/#subdebate-44-17)

Australia had no formal governmental relations with the three governments which as members of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> were effectively administering the Baltic States. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1975/19750602_reps_29_hor95/#subdebate-47-0)

* During question time the diplomats were asked whether it was true that women worked in all types of professions in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, and whether this was necessary. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1975/19750602_reps_29_hor95/#subdebate-47-0)

* One of the diplomats answered the questions very courteously by saying that more women worked in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> that probably in any other country in the world, the reason being that when they were at war as our allies against the tyranny of Nazi Fascism, so many of their men were in the fighting forces that it was necessary for the women to do the men's jobs. * The interesting thing is that this is the first time that members of this Parliament sitting opposite have taken such a viewpoint of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781121_reps_31_hor112/#debate-15)

* The Parliamentary delegation that went to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> could have been looked upon as one that was elected to comply with the wishes of the middle order official from the Soviet Embassy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781121_reps_31_hor112/#debate-16)

* The honourable member for Corio made an incorrect statement last week when he said that the Department of Foreign Affairs gave an undertaking to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> that no members of the Joint Foreign Affairs and Defence Subcommittee on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> would be included in any parliamentary delegation to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781121_reps_31_hor112/#debate-17)

* There are those with a genuine concern regarding the suppression of civil liberties, as epitomised by the honourable member for Prospect, and there are those who need to aspire to the desires of others who would seek to suppress criticism of the suppression of civil liberties in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, namely, the honourable member for Melbourne Ports  (Mr Holding)  who goes along with the socialists in Victoria who would not condemn the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> for its brutal suppression of civil liberties. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781121_reps_31_hor112/#debate-17)

* Some few moments ago in a speech to the House by the Minister for Foreign Affairs  (Mr Peacock)-  perhaps it was an exercise in the honourable gentleman's forensic skills- he described members of the Australian Labor Party as being of two kinds: Those who were genuinely concerned with problems of civil liberties and those who, to quote the Minister's words, were concerned to suppress evidence of oppression of dissident groups within the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781121_reps_31_hor112/#debate-35)

* Indeed, only this morning in another article in the  Australian Financial Review  I noticed that  Mr John  Silkin, the United Kingdom Minister for Agriculture, Food and Fisheries remarked on the fact that the EEC has sold subsidised butter to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> at a price of about 47.5 pence a pound compared with 60 pence a pound paid by British shoppers for the same product. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781123_reps_31_hor112/#subdebate-11-0)

* Without wishing to disclose the price that has been received in the recent sale of Australian butter to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> I think it is apparent that Australia's ability to sell agricultural produce in Third World markets is seriously prejudiced by the maintenance of the very high subsidies on European produce that is applied through the Common Agricultural Policy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781123_reps_31_hor112/#subdebate-11-0)

* -In recent months mankind right around the world has strongly and vociferously condemned the systematic persecution of civil rights dissidents in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781123_reps_31_hor112/#debate-34)

* On Remembrance Day 1978 a small section of the Australian community but an influential section of the Australian community not only chose to forget those who are fighting for basic human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, but they callously turned their backs on those freedom fighters in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, the modernday martyrs of 1978. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781123_reps_31_hor112/#debate-34)

* What a day of shame for Australia when one of the two major political parties in the State of Victoria came out publicly and refused to condemn the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> for its treatment of civil rights dissidents. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781123_reps_31_hor112/#debate-34)

* We have asked questions of the Minister particularly in relation to the Finnish Agreement and the fact that uranium will be enriched in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>- asking about safeguards procedures for toll enrichment- and we are not getting any assistance. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781124_reps_31_hor112/#subdebate-43-0)

* There is not much point in attacking the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> on the basis of having bugging devices here as though it is a pleasant exercise and in the same context not telling anything about nuclear safeguards arrangements with that country from the point of view of uranium supplied to Finland. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781124_reps_31_hor112/#subdebate-43-0)

* Has the EEC suspended export subsidies or restitutions on butter sales pending an inquiry into an attempted sale of French butter to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> contrary to the notification procedure introduced after a similar sale in 1 977. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1978/19781124_reps_31_hor112/#subdebate-58-98)

* Is he able to say what is (a) the number or nuclear power plants and (b) the nuclear electricity generating capacity of plants (i) in operation, (ii) under construction, (iii) planned or on order and (iv) planned or on order and subsequently cancelled or deferred during the last5 years in (A) the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, (B) Eastern Europe, (C) Cuba and (D) the People's Republic of China. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790220_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-56-26)

* It so happens that the Strategic Arms Limitation Talks II encompass the cruise missile involving the United States of America and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790221_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-15-0)

* It ought to be noted, I think, that the ANZUS treaty was emphasised in a very particular way last year because even though discussions were going on between the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and the United States about lowering force levels in the Indian Ocean- I have indicated that I hope those discussions can be resumed- a major ANZUS exercise involving significant United States and Australian forces took place off the coast of Western Australia in the Indian Ocean. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-3-0)

* Has that not pushed the Vietnamese into the arms of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* The Labor Government had good diplomatic relations with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* The Australian Government has failed to maintain a balance in relations with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> on the one hand and China on the other hand. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* It has made a strong effort to isolate Vietnam and it has helped to drive it straight towards the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* The ability of the Vietnam Government to absorb those problems is limited by the lack of assistance it received from other countries except of course the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and some socialist countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* It had no option but to sign a friendship treaty with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* We have some evidence of the sharpening of the differences within the Vietnamese leadership as the links with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are bound tighter and tighter. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790222_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-38-0)

* The conflicts reflect and were created by the hostility and rivalry existing among four states: The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, China, Vietnam and Kampuchea. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* I emphasise this deliberate and substantial militarisation of African conflict by outside states- particularly the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and its Cuban surrogates- because I do not think that the qualitative change it has wrought in African affairs has registered clearly enough. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* The situation began to deteriorate last year with increasing hostilities between Kampuchea and Vietnam, a worsening relationship between China and Vietnam and the signing of a Treaty of Friendship and Co-operation- which included a military assistance clause- between the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and Vietnam. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* The Vietnamese attack on Kampuchea was an attack by a client of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> on a client of China. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* Whatever its motivation the attack bore directly on the rivalry and competition between the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and China for long term influence in the region- and, more generally, on the whole Sino-Soviet dispute. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* China's subsequent incursion into Vietnam can only be understood as a reaction to Vietnam's treaty with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, its invasion of Kampuchea and the installation there of a pro- Vietnamese Government. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* In turn, its concern about events in Kampuchea relate not only to the extension of Vietnamese influence but also to the role of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> as Vietnam's principal -backer. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* We have called on Vietnam to withdraw its forces from Kampuchea, on China to withdraw its forces from Vietnam and on the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to exercise restraint to prevent the last turn of the screw, which could be disastrous not merely for the region but for the peace of the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* It is a neighbour of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, a major oil producer and a principal member of the Organisation of Petroleum Exporting Countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* While the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is increasing its already enormous military power faster than any other country, and while it is increasingly active in relation to the trouble spots of the world, politically it is the odd-man-out among the great powers. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-0)

* At the time of the Korean War, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> was pleased to see China at war and can welcome now in its own terms the dissipation of China's energy in the south. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> need not lift a finger in the sense that it may well hope that China's influence could fail. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is greatly advantaged by the Chinese operation in Vietnam. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> was delighted when China was embroiled in Korea in the 1950s and those qualities of spreading the interest and flexibility which so characterise Soviet policy are likely to be satisfied to see China at war with Vietnam and China's relations with Vietnam being shattered for a generation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The central elements of his arguments in relation to these various international elements can be linked with a decline in the power of the United States and the increase in the power of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Whilst all of us wish for nothing more than peace between nations regardless of differences of ideological approach, the reality facing us today is that we have seen, over the last few years in particular, a steady but sure increase in the military capacity of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> compared with the United States of America. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* It is so easy to imagine a situation where one mistake, one miscalculation, one rifle bullet across an international frontier, could well be enough to launch the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> against China- an action which would result, quite likely, in disastrous consequences for all of mankind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Our world today is a relatively small place and nations have the capacity, in the form of intercontinental ballistic missiles and manned bombers, to travel great distances, for example from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to Australia, or from the United States to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>- in fact virtually around the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Despite this enormous military build-up by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> in recent years, it must be recognised that since 1945 no Soviet unit has been placed in a military position against any other state. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In recent years there has not been one trouble spot, not even Northern Ireland, in which has not been found among the arsenal of those who wish to fight equipment supplied by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* For example, in the North Atlantic Treaty Organisation area of Western Europe there is again a degree of malaise in that the United States and its Western allies demonstrably do not have at this point of time at least equality of strategic capability with the Warsaw Pact countries, which include the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Cuban forces, armed and equipped by the Soviet, have again been prepared to be the catspaw of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, dabbling wherever possible in strife between states, in civil wars between rulers and people and between rulers and their own elite as in Chad. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In fact, we are seeing a pronounced deterioration in the relative strength of the United States and its allies visavis the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and its allies, a pronounced deterioration in the capacity of the Western alliance to present a united face, and a deterioration in the capacity of the Third World to feel that in the West it has a group of states which are reliable, can be depended upon to make decisions and have the courage to carry them out for the welfare of mankind. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* We commend the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> for its moderation in response to the Chinese actions, but it is to be regretted that the same moderating influence was not extended from Moscow in the case of Vietnam's actions against Kampuchea. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Co-operation with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> serves the cause of peace, for in the nuclear age world peace must include peace betweeen the superpowers- and it must mean the control of nuclear arms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* President Carter went on to say that SALT II will not be based on sentiment, but on the self interest of the United States and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Our relationship with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is a mixture of cooperation and competition, and as President of the United States, I have no more difficult task than to balance the two. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* It is in our national interest to pursue it even as we continue competition with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> elsewhere in the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* She has her own reasons for trying to marshal powerful forces against the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Frankly, it would suit China to see the United States with overwhelming weapons superiority over the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Yet, in fact, the United States is prepared in SALT II to accept numerical equality of nuclear weapons with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* If anyone were to suggest that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is not involved in any way in this matter and is just an innocent bystander wanting to assist wherever possible, he would be very naive indeed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* If one were to read the statements made by the foreign ministers of other great nations one would realise that there has been an obvious attempt in each case to try to appreciate a situation which involves the possibility of an unthinkable conflict, that is, the possibility of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and China coming into conflict. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The Australian Foreign Minister has made this statement at a time when continuous attempts are being made by the United States to achieve a genuine detente with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* I am not suggesting for one moment that they gave me classified information, but the general impression there is that America is getting nearer to a genuine understanding- and this is being achieved in a remarkable way- with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> at the same time as this very wonderful association is being built up with communist China. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* As people who have talked about the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> have said, we are dealing not with the dictatorship of the proletariat but with the dictatorship of the secretariat. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* There is a dictatorship in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and there is a dictatorship in many other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In some cases the difference may be only marginal such as in the disputes between the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and China or between Chile and Argentina. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* I raised the point that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> indicated to this country last year that it would invite a parliamentary delegation to visit that country only on the basis that no members of the Joint Foreign Affairs and Defence Sub-committee on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> would be on that delegation. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* This Government to its eternal shame agreed to send to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> a delegation on the basis that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> had decided that certain persons in this Parliament were persona non grata. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* For example, there would be no point in Australia deciding to boycott the Olympic Games to be held in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The Olympic Games would be held in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> even if Australia decided not to participate. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> would be able to say that a campaign was being conducted by countries opposed to the holding of the Games there. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* This would only be to the advantage of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* I would like to make this point in relation to the conflict in South East Asia: It is utter hypocrisy for the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to criticise China or the United States for interfering in other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has occupied- in some cases continually- nearly all of Eastern Europe. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In some cases- for example, the Baltic States- it has actually incorporated the countries into the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* With its Cuban mercenaries fighting in much of Africa, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has a hide to talk about interference in other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* One would imagine that if a direct request were made and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> attacked China in any force, the Chinese would neutralise their southern flank with a much, much heavier blow being directed at Vietnam than at present. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* I suppose that it is not in Vietnam's interest to call in aid from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> at this time. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In the world scene, it is perfectly clear that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is seeking to obtain strategic dominance throughout the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In 1985 the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> will have a strategic superiority over the United States of America that will be very, very pronounced. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* Therefore, at about that time there will be a predominance by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, which has shown itself willing to use client states to the utmost to achieve its strategic aims. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* That aim has been announced by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* When the honourable member for Dawson  (Mr Braithwaite)  and I paid a state visit to China in July 1978, we were both struck- and this is a highly bipartisan comment- by the widespread fear, which was expressed everywhere we went, about the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* In China at the moment there is enormous fear of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* I have been to China on two occasions in the last four years and I have been to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> as well. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The Chinese are fearful of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> detests the Chinese. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The United States, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and certainly Vietnam and Cambodia should be present as should some of the other great countries of the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19790227_reps_31_hor113/#subdebate-18-1)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is the only country in the world that can endanger world peace and the only country that has both the will and the ability to create a world diversion and involve the rest of the world in possible nuclear assault of one kind or another. * It may have a good deal more in common with the system of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791017_reps_31_hor116/#debate-32)

* We would have to go to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> or China to see a comparable concentration of media control. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791018_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-31-0)

* The Committee gave extensive consideration to the text ban question, but work on the drafting of a treaty awaits the conclusion of the discussions now under way among the United States, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and Britain. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* The United States and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> presented to the Committee a draft convention banning- radiological weapons. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> at that stage did not seem to have enough allies to enable Australia to get a place on the Committee. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* The Minister notes that this prospective treaty is currently the subject of negotiations between the two super-powers, namely, the United States and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* This is true, but even more to the point is that the achievement of a comprehensive test ban is dependent in the first instance on the conclusion of a new Strategic Arms Limitation Talks agreement between the United States and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* Firstly, without agreement on SALT II there is little prospect of the United States and the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> agreeing on any other arms control matter in the next few years. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* Secondly, unless the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and the United States agree on limitations to their own armaments, there is nil prospect of critically important countries, such as India, Pakistan, Brazil, Argentina and South Africa, agreeing to a comprehensive test ban. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791025_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-30-0)

* I point out in passing that the leading officials of the Building Workers Industrial Union have a very close association with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and strongly support the policies that that country pursues. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-8-0)

* -On behalf of the Joint Committee on Foreign AfFairs and Defence I present the Committee's report on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, together with the transcript of evidence. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -by leave-The report of the Joint Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence entitled 'Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>' is based on the evidence given to a sub-committee of the Joint Committee. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Many witnesses had extensive experience in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Nevertheless, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has failed to enter into the spirit of the Universal Declaration of Human Rights, and has failed to implement many of its formal commitments in such documents as the International Covenant on Civil and Political Rights and the Final Act of the 1975 Helsinki Agreement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Within three years of  Mr Brezhnev  signing the Final Act of the Helsinki Agreement, the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> flouted the Agreement's human rights provisions to such an extent that it has even imprisoned or expelled most of the people who, with considerable courage, had openly monitored the extent of Soviet compliance with the Helsinki Agreement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Soviet citizens may not engage in independent political activity, nor form or belong to political parties other than the Communist Party of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>; nor do the Soviet people have an opportunity to effect a change in their government or parliaments through the ballot box. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Union of Soviet Socialist Republics is unique among the major powers in that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>'s dominant nationality is portentially outnumbered. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The democratic movement in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has received some severe setbacks in recent years. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Many leading activists are now imprisoned for long terms, exiled to remote parts of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> or expelled abroad. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is systematically abusing psychiatry through the forced internment of mentally healthy people in order to cure them of their political or religious beliefs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* This also enables the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to avoid the presence of some important dissidents at trials. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Australia should be conscious of its respect for human rights in its relationship with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Similarly this can be done by individual Australians during cultural, academic and scientific exchanges with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* As the evidence before the Sub-Committee on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> was to a great extent unfavourable to the Soviet Government, the Committee regrets that the Soviet Embassy in Australia did not avail itself of ample formal or informal opportunities to put a Soviet viewpoint to the Sub-Committee. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -by leave-As a member of the Joint Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence but not a member of the Sub-Committee on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> I think it is important that the House take note of the fact that a number of dissenting reports have been published as well as the report which has just been tabled. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* They are not available in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -Before the suspension of the sitting I was speaking to the report on human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> which has been presented today. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* They do not indicate that there is not a denial of human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* My concern is that in undertaking an inquiry of the magnitude of this report into human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> no funds- I repeat, no funds- were made available for the Committee to enable it to ensure it had available to it those witnesses whom it sought in order to carry out its inquiries or inspections. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Certainly, an invitation was extended to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to give evidence. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I do not think that anyone of intelligence in this House would expect the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to appear before a jury in Australia to give evidence on its own affairs. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is not obliged to appear before such an inquiry and Australia is not obliged either. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is a restrictive and repressive regime as are those regimes throughout the world which are totalitarian in character. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Such regimes are not limited to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> but many do not profess to be libertarian or democratic. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The conditions exposed in this report deal with civil liberties in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Those I speak of are those responsible for the denial of those civil liberties in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -by leave-This report is an indictment against the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It documents the alleged devotion of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to human rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Whether or not Jews in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are the victims of adverse discrimination in citizenship, in rights to religious practice, in rights to publish, communicate, travel, emigrate and organise. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> bearing in mind Australia's support for the principles contained in the Universal Declaration of Human Rights and the final act of the Helsinki Agreement. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Included in those 25 witnesses were six who had served prison sentences in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>- for example, Pastor Grivans, who had graduated from the theological institute in Riga in 1928. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The human rights movement throughout the world was responsible for the ultimate release by the Soviet authorities of Leonid Plyushch and the permission which was granted to him to leave the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It will be clear to any reader of the transcript of the public evidence which is available, or from this report, that witnesses were called to give their evidence because of expertise on the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and its application of human rights, and not for their political allegiance or philosophy. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* If one examined the documents from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>- for example, the Soviet Constitutions of 1936 and 1977, the Helsinki Accords, the criminal code or the law on religious associations, and then took the evidence of former citizens of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> who suffered as a result of action by Soviet authorities pursuant to Soviet law, the Committee's conclusions are found to be soundly based. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* In the first place, I refer to the program of Russification adopted by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* If the political climate of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> does not change, then the consequence is likely to be the dilution of our nation in the sea of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Anti-semitic practices adopted in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are summarised in Chapter 5 of the report. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* In 1975 the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> signed the final act of the Helsinki Agreement, which states: [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* That is part of the Helsinki accords which were signed by the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> four years ago. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Committee received evidence, for example, that such literature is published outside the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and we had one case referred to us where an action was taken against the Soviet officials in the USSR Embassy in France to stop the dissemination of anti-semitic literature in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* On this particular matter the Committee recommends in paragraph 26 of the conclusions and recommendations that our Government should press the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to cease the circulation of any anti-semitic literature in this country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Committee found it difficult to understand Soviet thinking because there are many citizens of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> who practise the Jewish faith who are anxious to remain as citizens of that State and who wish to continue with Jewish cultural activities within the USSR. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I conclude by considering one matter which the Committee was careful to determine early in its deliberations and that is the question whether an investigation by a parliamentary committee into human rights in the USSR would have an adverse affect in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> on those people whom the Committee was anxious to support. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Almost without exception witness after witness confirmed that the Committee's actual hearing, let alone its final report and recommendation, was of considerable assistance to those within the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> who were seeking to establish human rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* In the course of his examination, I asked whether protests by lawyers or legal institutions in Australia would have any influence on the denial of due process of law in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* When Professor Telford Taylor has criticised the proceedings that have been conducted in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, and particularly in many of the Jewish dissident cases, I think it is important, although they deny that it makes any impact upon them. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* He referred in particular to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> being a super power which, because of the enunciation of the rights of Soviet citizens in the Constitution, wants the world to believe that those rights are enjoyed by every citizen in that country. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The  Chairman  would also say that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is an 'evangelising super power' seeking to persuade people outside the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> that the USSR model is one which should be followed in other nations. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It would be also my wish that every member of the Red Army Russian Song and Dance Company, presently touring Australia, could return to their homeland with a copy of the human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> report made to this Parliament. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* This report should be compulsory reading for every visitor, sportsman and woman and official who will visit the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> for the 1980 Moscow Olympics. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* This report should be read by all people interested in the freedom of the individual and by those who seek to understand how society operates in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* As a member of the Sub-Committee of the Joint Committee on Foreign Affairs and Defence which prepared the report on human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, I would like to make a few points. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has only one political party. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* That is why the present position in respect of human rights exists in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, as illustrated in this report. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I make one point in relation to human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and in relation to the nationality question: I do not necessarily support nationalistic claims, whether they be by people who originated in the Baltic States or in the Ukraine, those of Jews and so on and tend to oppose nationalism. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I think that it is important to have democratic freedom in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* But what is happening at the present time is that they can neither change the setup inside the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> nor leave the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I would like to make a couple of points about human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I think that those of us who have been interested in the question of freedom and the question of human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and in other countries know- the report emphasises it in its first conclusions- that there have been positive changes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* In other words, changes have occurred in some ways away from the extreme totalitarian state of what was generally considered to be a Stalinist society in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> until the death of Stalin. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* But it is still important to know what is happening in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> at the present time. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* He has a very intelligent approach to what is happening in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It was certainly a pleasant change from the usual content of  Broadband  programs on the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and its satellites. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I hope that it will stimulate discussion on the question of civil liberties not only in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> but in other countries. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -Following on from what was said by the previous  speaker,  the honourable member for Prospect  (Dr Klugman),  I have never asked for a visa to visit the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, or any country associated with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, either in Europe or in Asia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Committee has aimed in its report on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to present an objective, factual body of material. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* From this information the Committee has drawn a number of conclusions which to a large extent are based on the testimony of witnesses whom the SubCommittee on Human Rights had sought due to their personal experience in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Other speakers have outlined the justification for the production of the report on human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and some of its findings. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* A major area in which the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> represses human rights concerns ethnic minorities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* As emphasised in the report there is State interference in almost all religious activity in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> will need to pay great attention to the aspirations of its large Muslim communities. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* A further example of repression of human rights is the restriction on a citizen's intention to permanently move to another part of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* There have been some successful campaigns outside the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> to secure the release or emigration of imprisoned Soviet intellectuals and dissidents, or on behalf of those threatened with imprisonment. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* One of the most notable international efforts to counter human rights violations in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has been the campaign against Soviet abuse of psychiatry for political purposes. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The report makes several recommendations on what the West can do to secure improved human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* As long as the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> seeks goodwill and economic concessions from the West, there seems to be scope for the West to achieve a more humane Soviet attitude towards its own people. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Australia should insist that a regard for human rights be part of Australia's relationship with the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> sometimes claims a lack of understanding in the West of its case on human rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Committee has recommended that the Australian Government suggest to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> that it may be possible to arrange a reciprocal exchange of views in the Soviet and Australian newspapers and in other publications. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* That may seem to some to be an unrealistic suggestion and I doubt that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> will take it up. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Furthermore, it is recommended that Australia seek the right to distribute informative publications in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, in the same way that the USSR is allowed to distribute in Australia. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> of course is not the only offender regarding the violation of human rights; there are some other nations where attention needs to be directed. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* However, the substance of this particular report is directed to the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and therefore that is where the original charge lies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We would reiterate our view that based on the substantial evidence available the civil rights of certain groups,  especially minorities, in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are seriously infringed and fall below that which should be expected in any civilised society. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* For those reasons, whilst I accept completely that there are infringements of civil rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, I am one of those who feel that the recommendation in paragraph 65 and the original reference of the matter to the SubCommittee can do untold harm to Australia in the future. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* -As a member of the Sub-Committee on Human Rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, which undertook this inquiry, I want to speak for a few moments on this subject. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* We are concerned here with civil rights not only in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> but also throughout the world. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I shall read part of the Reservations that was expressed because we did not hear evidence from the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* It is realised that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> was asked to provide contrary evidence and refused to do so. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Above all, the important aspect of this document is that a group of members from both sides of this Parliament was given the responsibility to look into human rights in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* I am depressed that suspicion of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> has increased over the last few years, and likewise <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> suspicion of the rest of the world, particularly the West, has also increased. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* But, one would have to be blind to not recognise that inside the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> there are great deprivations of human rights. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* First of all, why pick the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>? [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* One has to say that the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> is powerful, influential and stable. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* Having been there, I can say quite emphatically that one feels safe and secure wherever one travels in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> now has some of the problems of the rest of the world in regard to these matters but, it does have freedoms. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* So far as one can tell, the people of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> are free of the real poverty that inflicts a great number of other societies. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* That is obviously not the case in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* The Chilean Government, which I think would be much worse than that of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, permitted the inquiry to go ahead. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791108_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-41-0)

* This compares with 83,000 million tonnes in the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and 1 14,000 million tonnes in the United States. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791114_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-38-2)

* There is the potential that the situation there may lead to further conflict between China and Vietnam, which in turn could possibly involve the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> in the area. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791120_reps_31_hor116/#debate-46)

* The potential influence of the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span>, using its surrogate, Cuba, for disruption in the internal affairs of Africa, has caused considerable concern both on the continent and elsewhere. [[More&hellip;]](https://historichansard.net/hofreps/1979/19791120_reps_31_hor116/#subdebate-47-0)

* The Government took the view that the situation then existing in southern Africa was morally wrong, and we believed that it would only enhance the interests and activities of hostile outside nations, including the <span class="highlight">Soviet Union</span> and its supporters.
